* beta[None,:,:]).sum(axis=(1,2)), 1e-12)\n    alpha_new = np.clip(alpha_new, 1e-12, None)\n    beta_new = y.sum(axis=0) / np.maximum((n * alpha_new[:,None])[:,:,None].sum(axis=0), 1e-12)\n    beta_new = np.clip(beta_new, 1e-12, None)\n    da = np.max(np.abs(np.log(alpha_new/alpha)))\n    db = np.max(np.abs(np.log(beta_new/beta)))\n    alpha, beta = alpha_new, beta_new\n    if max(da,db) < 1e-12:\n        break\n\nmu = n[:,:,None] * alpha[:,None,None] * beta[None,:,:]\nobs = y.sum(axis=1)\nexp = mu.sum(axis=1)\nresid = (obs-exp)/np.sqrt(np.maximum(exp,1e-12))\nratio = (obs+1e-9)/(exp+1e-9)\nrows=[]\nfor c in cities:\n    for k in cats:\n        i,j = ci[c], ki[k]\n        rows.append((c,k,obs[i,j],exp[i,j],resid[i,j],ratio[i,j]))\nres = pd.DataFrame(rows, np.max(np.abs(np.log(beta_new/beta)))) < 1e-12:\n            alpha, beta = alpha_new, beta_new\n            break\n        alpha, beta = alpha_new, beta_new\n    mu = n[:,:,None] * alpha[:,None,None] * beta[None,:,:]\n    obs = y.sum(axis=1)\n    exp = mu.sum(axis=1)\n    resid = (obs-exp)/np.sqrt(np.maximum(exp,1e-12))\n    rows=[]\n    for c in cities:\n        for k in cats:\n            i,j = u=u[u['is_active']]\nmajor=u['city'].value_counts(); major=major[major>=85].index.tolist(); u=u[u['city'].isin(major)]\nleaf=pd.read_csv('category_001.csv'); leaf=leaf[leaf['parent_category_id']\"'!=0][['\"'category_id','category_name']]\nlistings=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f,usecols=['listing_id','category_id']) for f in sorted(glob('listing_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True)\ncities=sorted(major); types=sorted(u['user_type'].unique()); cats=sorted(leaf['category_name'].unique())\nci={c:i for i,c in enumerate(cities)}; ti={t:i for i,t in enumerate(types)}; ki={k:i for i,k in enumerate(cats)}\nN=np.zeros((len(cities),len(types)))\nfor (c,t),g in u.groupby(['city','user_type']): N[ci[c],ti[t]]=len(g)\n\ndef residuals(events):\n    Y=np.zeros((len(cities),len(types),len(cats)))\n    for (c,t,k),g in events.groupby(['city','user_type','category_name']): Y[ci[c],ti[t],ki[k]]=len(g)\n    alpha=np.ones(len(cities)); break\n        alpha,beta=anew,bnew\n    MU=N[:,:,None]*alpha[:,None,None]*beta[None,:,:]\n    obs=Y.sum(axis=1); exp=MU.sum(axis=1); resid=(obs-exp)/np.sqrt(np.maximum(exp,1e-12))\n    rows=[]\n    for c in cities:\n        for k in cats:\n            i,j=ci[c],ki[k]\n            rows.append((c,k,resid[i,j]))\n    return pd.DataFrame(rows, columns=['city','category','resid'])\n\np = pd.read_csv('purchase_001.csv', usecols=['buyer_id','listing_id']).merge(u[['user_id','city','user_type']], left_on='buyer_id', right_on='user_id').merge(listings,on='listing_id').merge(leaf,on='category_id')\ns = pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f,usecols=['user_id','category_id']) for f in sorted(glob('search_event_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True).merge(u[['user_id','city','user_type']], on='user_id').merge(leaf,on='category_id')\ncl = pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f,usecols=['user_id','listing_id']) for f in sorted(glob('click_event_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True).merge(u[['user_id','city','user_type']], on='user_id').merge(listings,on='listing_id').merge(leaf,on='category_id')\nf = pd.read_csv('favorite_event_001.csv', usecols=['user_id','listing_id']).merge(u[['user_id','city','user_type']], on='user_id').merge(listings,on='listing_id').merge(leaf,on='category_id')\nres = residuals(p).rename(columns={'resid':'p'}).merge(residuals(s).rename(columns={'resid':'s'}),on=['city','category']).merge(residuals(cl).rename(columns={'resid':'c'}),on=['city','category']).merge(residuals(f).rename(columns={'resid':'f'}),on=['city','category'])\nres['mean'] = res[['p','s','c','f']].mean(axis=1)\nres['median'] = res[['p','s','c','f']].median(axis=1)\nfor th in [-3.5,-3.2,-3.0,-2.8,-2.7,-2.6,-2.5,-2.4]:\n    print('mean<',th, (res['mean']<th).sum(), 'median<',th, (res['median']<th).sum())\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}
